## Analysis

The Ground Truth expression is:
$$GT = 0.79911 \cdot A^{1/3} - 0.49947 \cdot A - 0.49947 \cdot A \cdot e^{-0.05057t}$$

The key structural components are:
1. A term proportional to $A^{1/3}$ (fractional power of A)
2. A term proportional to $A$ (linear in A, constant in t)
3. A term proportional to $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$ (linear in A, exponential decay in t)

For a candidate to match, it must be able to reproduce:
- The $A^{1/3}$ term
- The $A$ term (constant in t)
- The $A \cdot \exp(\text{negative constant} \cdot t)$ term
- No other non-zero terms

Let me check candidates that contain $A^{c}$ (power term) and $A \cdot \exp(ct)$ type terms:

**Candidate 1**: Has $A^{c4} \cdot c5$ but also $c6 \cdot t/(c7+t)$ and $c8 \cdot \exp(c9 \cdot t)$ — no $A \cdot \exp(ct)$ term. The exponential term doesn't have A multiplied. Cannot produce $A \cdot e^{-\alpha t}$.

**Candidate 14**: $A^2 c_0 + A^2 c_1 + Ac_2 + Ac_3 + A^{c4}c_5 \exp(c_6 t) + c_7 \exp(c_8 t)$. This has $A^{c4}c_5\exp(c_6 t)$ — the power term is multiplied by exponential in t, not separated. Setting $c_6=0$ gives $A^{c4}c_5$ (constant), but then there's no $A\cdot\exp(ct)$ term. The $c_7\exp(c_8 t)$ doesn't have A. Cannot match.

**Candidate 22**: $A^2 c_0 + Ac_1 + Ac_2 t\exp(c_3 t) + A^{c4}c_5 + c_6 t/(c_7+t) + c_8\exp(c_9 t)$. Has $A^{c4}c_5$ for the $A^{1/3}$ term and $Ac_1$ for the $-0.5A$ term, but the time-dependent A term is $Ac_2 t\exp(c_3 t)$, not $A\exp(ct)$. Cannot match since $t\exp(ct) \neq \exp(ct)$.

**Candidate 37**: $Ac_0 + Ac_1/(A+c_2) + A^{c3}c_4 + c_5 t\exp(c_6 t) + c_7 + c_8\exp(c_9 t)$. Has $A^{c3}c_4$ for $A^{1/3}$, but no $A\cdot\exp(ct)$ term.

**Candidate 38**: $A^2 c_0 + A^2 c_1 \exp(Ac_2) + Ac_3 + A^{c4}c_5 + c_6 t/(c_7+t) + c_8\exp(c_9 t)$. Setting $c_0=0, c_1=0$ removes A² terms. Has $Ac_3$ and $A^{c4}c_5$. But the exponential $c_8\exp(c_9 t)$ doesn't multiply A. Cannot produce $A\cdot\exp(-\alpha t)$.

**Candidate 42**: $A^{c0}c_1\exp(c_2 t) + A^{(c_3+c_4 t)}c_5 + c_6\exp(c_7 t)$. Setting $c_0=1$ gives $Ac_1\exp(c_2 t)$ for the $A\exp(-\alpha t)$ term. The second term $A^{c_3+c_4 t}$ — setting $c_4=0, c_3=1/3$ gives $A^{1/3}c_5$. And $c_6\exp(c_7 t)$ with $c_6=0$ removes it. But we still need the $-0.5A$ term (constant × A). There's no pure $A$ term available. Cannot match.

**Candidate 44**: $A^2 c_0/(A+c_1)^2 + Ac_2 + A^{(c_3+c_4 t)}c_5 + c_6\exp(c_7 t)$. Setting $c_4=0, c_3=1/3$ gives $A^{1/3}c_5$. Has $Ac_2$ for the linear term. But $A^2/(A+c_1)^2$ with $c_0=0$ removes it, and $c_6\exp(c_7 t)$ doesn't have A factor. No $A\cdot\exp(ct)$ term.

After exhaustive analysis, no candidate can simultaneously produce $A^{1/3}$, $A$, and $A\cdot e^{-\alpha t}$ with no residual terms.

Conclusion: No match
